if ('PerformanceObserver' in window) {
  const observer = new PerformanceObserver(list => {
    for (const entry of list.getEntries()) {
      if (['first-paint', 'first-contentful-paint'].includes(entry.name)) {

}

  <script>
   function canUseLocalStorage() {
  var t = "t";
  try {
    localStorage.setItem(t, t);
    localStorage.removeItem(t);
    return true;
  } catch (e) {
    return false;
  }
}

function hasFeature(name) {
  const searchParams = new URLSearchParams(location.search)
  const activeFeaturesString = searchParams.get('features') || ''
  const activeFeaturesList = activeFeaturesString.split(',')
  return activeFeaturesList.includes(name)
}

function isValidId(id) {
  var ID_Length = 10
  var reg = /^[0-9]+.[0-9]+$/g
  return id.split('').length > ID_Length && reg.test(id)
}
